<UserId.>109933404675083013986< /UserId.><name>Shawn Silverman< /name><Time>1531624261140</Time><Rate>5</Rate>< review>
I highly recommend this place if you're really hungry. The all you can eat and the all you can eat AND drink deals are amazing. The spicy miso broth and ginger chicken are the famous broths (order half and half to get both). If it's your first time to shabu/hot pot you can always ask for help or read the instructions on the plastic table sign. They have other food items for those that are not really adventurous. Great location and easily commutable.</review>

<review>The name of the restaurant is ‚Äúlost‚Äù in the translation. The Chinese name is ‚ÄúÊùé‰∏ÄÂ≠£ÁîüÁÖéÈ¶Ü‚Äù. Presumably, ‚ÄúÊùé‰∏ÄÂ≠£‚Äù is the name of the owner. ‚ÄúÁîüÁÖé‚Äù is a type of Shanghainese style pan fried dumpling. ‚ÄúÈ¶Ü‚Äù means restaurant. So, this is a place mainly for eating the pan fried dumplings. Being a native Shanghainese, I must say that their dumplings are very good, or at least among one of the best in the Bay Area. Their dumplings are full of savory juice that can burn your tongue when the dumplings are hot. So be careful when eating. Remember, you do not want to wait till the dumplings are cool before eating since the juice will mostly be absorbed by the flour skin by then.

Due to current Covid 19 situation, I can only order dumplings to go. It‚Äôs about 15 minute drive to my house and the dumplings are still hot enough to devour. < Review>
Great Shanghai style cuisine at reasonable prices. Portion sizes are reasonable and the overall taste of their dishes is pretty good and spot on. Recommend the #1 Shanghai dumpling (similar to xiao long bao but with a crunchy bun exterior - careful not to burn yourself) and the Shrimp and Pork wonton soup. For those unfamiliar with Shanghai cuisine, it tends to have a semi-sweet and savory to sweet profile.</Review>

< Review>
I think Driven is one of the most overlooked entertainment facilities in the Bay area and one of Rohnert Parks best kept secrets. For fun , excitement and the thrill of the chase , Driven is unequivocally at the top of the heap. Available for parties , business gatherings , grudge racing or just a fun day behind the wheel of a surprisingly powerful , smog free racing cart , Driven is fully capable of delivering white knuckle excitement as well as some relaxing activities like miniature golf and a video game arcade . They also have a great cafe with pizza , burgers and lots of snacks to appease the hunger your surely gonna have from all that racing excitement.</Review>

After the first race which was relatively quick we were waiting for about an hour and a half then we asked when our next race was. Come to find out were weren't booked for any races afterward. So we waiting another half an hour for the second race and by that time 5:30 in the afternoon I just didnt feel like waiting anymore. I'm not sure if this is how it usually is or if things got messed up, just left with a bad taste in my mouth. I'm not saying I'll never come back either dont get me wrong, it just sucks that it was dealt with poorly and I dont feel too good about it.< /Review>

< review>
Karting here is fast and competitive, they provide a helmet and head sock, so great karting experience.  However, the arcade is terrible and the food court is often unmanned.  They have glow-in-the-dark mini-golf, which is cool but the course is short.  If you want a good arcade and mini-golf experience, go to Scandia just south on Redwood Dr., but the karting here is way better than Scandia's.</review>

<pics>None< /pics><Review>I have to concur with the other reviews here about weak customer service and general out-of-touch nature of their order and customer service phone team.  I have ordered probably a half dozen times from these guys and two times they processed the order online and charged my card without having product in stock. This is for items that were in stock on their website. Worse yet when I phoned days later to find out about my order and when it would ship, this is when they would say "we're out of stock", to which I reply "why didn't you call or email me?" and their response "we were just about to do that".  Right.
And don't expect the most friendly phone service either. It can range from okay to rather stiff & unfriendly.

This is not how you run a business. If your website doesn't handle real-time inventory, then it's either time to get a new website that does (like other suppliers) or get a better customer service department that is on top of this stuff to immediately alert the customer to a backorder, not wait for me to call first after you've charged my card & I've lost valuable days waiting for product. Every other bottle supplier I can think of in the USA has a website that handles inventory and will not allow you to place an order when stuff is out of stock. Heck GoDaddy has a shopping cart website with inventory control for $29/mo so its not like they can't afford it.   This is pure laziness or greed on the part of this company that either 1) doesn't want to deal with this issue, or 2) is content to take your order and run your card in hopes they can scramble to find product for you so they don't lose your business.  Bottom line, this is not a good practice and other bottle suppliers don't operate this way.
I will pay more to order from competitors knowing that I've got service included and I can count on product being shipped when ordered or being alerted otherwise.
One other thing - if you have a CPU order (customer pick up) plan on waiting, and waiting. Sure you'll save on freight but unless its a huge order it won't be worth your time hanging out in the parking lot amidst other customers waiting for the same thing. Also have not had this experience picking up elsewhere, will calls are usually quick and easy at most places without the long wait.
Management can post replies to these reviews all they want, but there's a reason people are saying the same thing over and over.

Great place if you're not in a hurry for product and don't require even average customer service.<//Review></record>

<rating>5< /rating>< review>
I walked into the store and the sales person, Kat, allowed me to come in, take a look around and then approached me and asked if she could help me. It was a pleasure to not be pressured. She listened to what I was looking for and then described to me the different types of mattresses. She then led me to the Bed Match diagnostic system that matches you with the mattresses best suited for your body type and sleep position. Kat brought me to each mattress I was matched with, describing the brand, type and construction, etc. She asked me to lay down for as long as I liked, leaving me alone to assume my ‚Äúsleep position‚Äù, but always keeping an eye on me for when I would sit up or if I had a question for her. Kat is extremely knowledgeable, knowing every product she introduced me to. She answered all of my questions, gave me room to go back and forth between mattresses and never pressured me for a decision. I chose the mattress I wanted, asked her about the pillows, and after her answer, I asked her to include 2 in my purchase. She offered the mattress protector and cover, telling me what it does and why it‚Äôs a good idea. She gave me a discount on the cover and included covers for my pillows. I made the purchase and look forward to my mattress and pillows being delivered. I am extremely pleased with the service I received from Kat. I highly recommend her to anyone looking to purchase a quality mattress from a quality store with a high quality sales person who will handle you with courtesy and respect.< /review>

<Review>My husband and I have been shopping for a new fifth wheel for over a year.  Our requirements were a little unique, as I needed a functioning office space because I work from home.  Also, this is going to be my husband's home for 5 days out of the week for the next 4 months, so we wanted a rig that was rated for full-time living.  Most of the rigs we saw may have had a bonus room, but the desk space was too small, or there were too many steps between the living room, down to the kitchen, back up to the bedroom and bathroom.  We're not old, but going up and down like that does take a toll on your knees.  Also, I wanted the solid stairs in and out of the rig, so that was consideration as well.

We had finally settled on a Keystone Montana 3854BR that has a bonus room w/ loft and outside kitchen.  It had residential appliances, theater seating, a full couch that can pull out into a bed, a love seat in the office which can also pull out into a bed, and full wall-to-wall desk - what a luxury!   When we finally went to find one, most of the RV dealers didn't have that model in stock.  We found one at Camping World in Bakersfield.  It had all the extras we wanted, including a king bed and a tow-hitch for the travel trailer.  My husband contacted them and worked with Virgil to negotiate a great price.  The best part?  Virgil even took our calls during his day off.  That's service.  Once we put the $500 down to secure the rig, I worked with Leesa for the financing.  She gave us all the information, and negotiated an excellent interest rate, lower than the one our credit union was offering.

The day we went to pick up the rig, it was cleaned and Bennie in service provided us excellent instruction about the ins and outs of the rig.  He was patient, knowledgeable, and his team fixed the small nits I pointed out right there and then.  Trust me, we went over that rig with a fine toothed comb - testing all the gadgets, the lights, the pop-outs, and my husband toured the roof and examined the exterior, the storage space, the mechanics of the rig very carefully.  Bennie didn't blink an eye, and was happy to help us with all of our questions and concerns.

When we went to financing with Leesa, she was very friendly, very patient with all our questions, very honest and upfront about what were responsible for, what the warranty covered and how long the warranty was good for.  The discrepancy between the packages was minimal given the excellent interest rate she negotiated, so we went with the platinum package warranty.

The Camping World at Bakersfield also has a full-service store, and we were able to get sheets and other essentials for the rig before we left.  We had a great experience with the crew and staff at this Camping World location.  No one pushed us into a sale, Virgil did not call us constantly and Leesa was responsive to my emails before we arrived at the site.  Other dealers had their sales people call and text us mercilessly, and while I understand they want to make a sale, they have to understand that spending $80K is a big decision and needs to be thought through carefully.  I felt the staff at Camping World Bakersfield understood this and provided us the time and comfort to make that decision while still being available to answer all our questions until final sale.  It was important to us to find a dealer that we felt comfortable with because we anticipate upgrading or purchasing at least one more rig in the future, and I'm glad to know we can come back to Camping World Bakersfield to get the kind of personal customer service we desire to find the perfect rig.  Thank you.<//Review>< Name>

<Review>We are first time RV owners so it was a pleasant surprise when we went to Camping World. No pesky sales people! There were sales people, but it was more like they were there to answer any questions and guide us through choosing the right RV for US.

Glenn was very open and honest. He explained everything about owning an RV and told us what our truck could pull and what it couldn't. It took us about a couple of weeks to decide which one we wanted, even changing our minds at the last moment for different one.

The "inside" staff (front desk, financial, store, parts, service, etc...) were just as fantastic. Everyone was so sweet and ready to help. If someone couldn't answer a question, they went and found someone who could.

The financial wizard, Leesa, was a darling and talked to us about all things financial and helped us go through the details of financing the RV. She was very patient and very friendly. When our indecision got the best of us, she didn't get frustrated. She laughed and came with us and saw two of the RV's that we were hemming and hawing over. She gave us some sound advice about payment over the one we decided we really wanted (but could we afford it?... Turns out we could!) So she helped our final decision.

All in all, my wife and I would highly recommend Camping World. Our experience has been nothing but great. We're extremely satisfied. < Review>
My wife and I purchased a 17' Jayco Baja Edition from here about 1 month ago.  We LOVE this trailer!
Mike Osgood greeted us promptly, and went straight to the trailers we were interested.  We looked at about 5, until we found the one we purchased.
Unlike a couple of other RV Centers, Mike was the first salesman, who Really knew the products.  There was absolute No pressure, and he let us take our time while looking at each trailer.  Other places made us feel rushed, but not here.
This is my first trailer purchase, so I had allot of questions, and Mike was terrific!  He explained everything I wanted to know about each unit, advantages, and disadvantages; he really knew his stuff!
Once in the sales office, we worked the numbers exactly to our liking.  It was one of the smoothest, and most pleasant buying experiences I've had.  My wife liked one of the chairs in the showroom, so Mike threw it into the deal.  Friendly, professional, knowledgeable, and listened to our needs.
After our great experience with Mike, we were off to finance, with Leesa.  She also was great!  She also is Very friendly, knowledgeable, and no pressure.  We were very excited about our purchase; Mike, and Leesa made it that much more fun, with no bs, providing a low key sales experience.
While we were in Finance, they were cleaning up our trailer, and installing the trailer brake unit on our SUV.  Ken than showed us to our trailer, which was now immaculate.  He started at the rear bumper, and explained everything we needed to know about our new trailer.  He answered every question, sometimes twice, as again, this was our first trailer purchase.  Very friendly, and knew our unit inside and out.
We took the trailer out that day, and used it for 3 days, near Morro Bay, Ca., without a hitch.
There was one problem.  The generator we purchased didn't start.  I called Camping World, and Spoke with Pam.  I was expecting a hassle, since everything else went so well.  She told me she was sorry for the inconvenience, and had me come in, and exchange the generator for another, which I did.  I'm sorry if anyone has experienced any problem here with sales, because our experience was so positive!
A wonderful buying experience, so different from many other places we visited.  We recommend them, without reservation.  See Mike, he's fantastic!< /Review>

We bought a new refrigerator for our 32 year old class c motorhome at this location and had them install it. They also installed a new exterior refrigerator access cover. All of this work was done this Memorial Day, while we waited.
